function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

}

<script language="JavaScript">
function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;
var getSmsBtn = $('#getSmsBtn');
var mobcheckcode = $('#mobcheckcode');

var intervalid ;
var countdowntime ;
var time = 60;
var ifMoreReActivate=false;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

//提示问题答案检查
//重写 by 郑弋天 20130621
$('.JS_checkInput').blur(function(){
	checkAnswer($(this));
});
function checkAnswer($ipt){
	var val = $ipt.val(),
		$tip = $ipt.siblings('.JS_tip'),
		isDate = $ipt.attr('data-isd')
	;
	if(getStrLength(val) < 1 || getStrLength(val) > 30){
		$tip.text('答案需为1到30位');
		$tip.css('display', 'inline-block');
		return false;
	}else{
    	$tip.hide();
    }
    return true;

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

}

<script language="JavaScript">
function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;
var getSmsBtn = $('#getSmsBtn');

var intervalid ;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

//提示问题答案检查
//重写 by 郑弋天 20130621
$('.JS_checkInput').blur(function(){
	checkAnswer($(this));
});
function checkAnswer($ipt){
	var val = $ipt.val(),
		$tip = $ipt.siblings('.JS_tip'),
		isDate = $ipt.attr('data-isd')
	;
	if(getStrLength(val) < 1 || getStrLength(val) > 30){
		$tip.text('答案需为1到30位');
		$tip.css('display', 'inline-block');
		return false;
	}else{
    	$tip.hide();
    }
    return true;
    // else if(isDate == 'true'){
    //     if (!/^\d{8}$/.test(val)) {
    //         $tip.text('请输入日期，例如“19910101”');
    //         $tip.css('display', 'inline-block');
    //         return false;
    //     }else{
    //         $tip.hide();
    //     }
    // }else if(isDate == 'false' && (!(isChinese(val) || isAlphabet(val)))){

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;
var getSmsBtn = $('#getSmsBtn');

var countdowntip = $('#countdowntip');
var sendSmsTip = $('#sendSmsTip');

var countdowntime ;
var time = 60;
var ifMoreReActivate=false;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

}

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

<script language="JavaScript">
function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;
var getSmsBtn = $('#getSmsBtn');
var mobcheckcode = $('#mobcheckcode');
var countdowntip = $('#countdowntip');

var intervalid ;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

function checkAnswer($ipt){

		$tip = $ipt.siblings('.JS_tip'),
		isDate = $ipt.attr('data-isd')
	;
	if(getStrLength(val) < 1 || getStrLength(val) > 30){
		$tip.text('答案需为1到30位');
		$tip.css('display', 'inline-block');
		return false;
	}else{
    	$tip.hide();
    }

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>

function init(){

		document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
        document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";

        var liOtppass=document.getElementById("li_otppass")
		if(liOtppass!=null) {
			liOtppass.style.display = "none";

		}
}

function checkChange(obj){
    if(obj){
        var value = obj.value;

         var liQuestion1=document.getElementById("li_question1");
         var liQuestion2=document.getElementById("li_question2");
         var liQuestion3=document.getElementById("li_question3");
         var answer1=document.getElementById("li_answer1");
         var answer2=document.getElementById("li_answer2");
         var answer3=document.getElementById("li_answer3");
         var answers=document.getElementById("li_answer_slide");
        if(value == "1"){
            document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "";
            document.getElementById("noFeeSmsList").style.display = "";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "none";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "none";

					answer1.style.display = "none";
		       		answer2.style.display = "none";
		       		answer3.style.display = "none";
                    answers.style.display = "none";
				}
        }else if(value == "2"){
           	document.getElementById("li_getSmsBtn").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("li_mobcheckcode").style.display = "none";

				if(liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null||liQuestion1!=null) {
					liQuestion1.style.display = "";
					liQuestion2.style.display = "";
					liQuestion3.style.display = "";

		       		answer1.style.display = "";
		       		answer2.style.display = "";
		       		answer3.style.display = "";
                    answers.style.display = "";
		    	}
        }
    }
}

var leftime;
var getSmsBtn = $('#getSmsBtn');

var countdowntip = $('#countdowntip');
var sendSmsTip = $('#sendSmsTip');

var countdowntime ;
var time = 60;
var ifMoreReActivate=false;

$(document).ready(function(){
		$(".t_iselect").iSelect().bind("i.change", function(){
		// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin

		if($(this).attr("val") == "1"){
			$(".unfeeObj").show();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
		}else{
			$(".unfeeObj").hide();
			$("#feeSmsList").hide();
			$("#nextBtn").show();
		}

		// -- end


			checkChange($(this).find("input:hidden")[0]);
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").blur(function(){
			if(!this.value){
				$("#mobileHolder").removeClass("hide");
			}
		});
		$("#mobcheckcode").focus(function(){
			$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
		});
		 getSmsBtn.bind('click',function(){
			sendMessage();
		});
		init();


		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		window.isAutoSend && sendMessage("notSend");
		// -- end

});

function sendMessage(param){
	var href = window.location.href;
	var protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0)
		protocol = "https";
	$.ajax({
   		type: "POST",
   		async : false,
   		url: protocol + "://reg.163.com/services/sendsms4login",
   		//data:{channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'},
		// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
		data: (function(){
			var p = {channel:'mibao2_replacemobile'};
			param==="notSend" && (p.isNotSend = "1");
			return p;
		})(),
		// -- end
   		success:onSuccess
	});
}

}

//取字符串长度，中文算2个字符
function getStrLength(str){
	var chineseRegex = /[^\x00-\xff]/g;
	var strLength = str.replace(chineseRegex,"**").length;
	return strLength;
}

//汉字校验
function isChinese(str)
{
	var reg=/^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//中文校验成功
		return true;
	}else
	{
		return false;
	}
}
//英文校验
function isAlphabet(str)
{
	var reg=/^[abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ]+$/i;
	if(reg.test(str))
	{//英文校验成功
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function count(){
	if(countdowntime == 0){
		clearInterval(intervalid);
		getSmsBtn.show();
		countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','');
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML','');
		countdowntime = time;
		return;
	}
	countdowntip.attr('innerHTML','还有<span style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; margin:0 3px; color:red;">' + countdowntime + '</span>秒可以再次获取验证码');
	countdowntime = countdowntime - 1;
}

function onSuccess(msg){
	var tip = '';
	if(msg == '200\n'){
		tip = '短信验证码发送成功，请注意查收';
	}else if(msg == '501\n'){
		tip = '您获取验证码次数过多，请改天再试';
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}

	// 2013-11-08 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if (msg.indexOf('501') !== -1 && msg.split(",").length === 3) {
		var arr = msg.split(",");
		$(".unfeeObj").hide();
		var htmlStr = '<div class="fm_left">短信验证：</div><div class="fm_right"><div>请您用手机编辑短信<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[1]+'</strong>发送到<strong style="color:#f00;">'+arr[2]+'</strong>。<br>然后点"已经发送"按钮。</div><br /><span id="isCheckedErr" style="display:none; padding-left:26px;background:url(/gaiban/images/errIcon.png) no-repeat 0 -3px;color:red;"></span><br /><span class="f_btn"><a href="javascript:void(0);" class="r_btn" id="hasSendBtn">已经发送</a></span><span id="isChecking" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/loading2.gif" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 正在验证中，请稍候。</span><span id="isCheckedOk" style="display:none;"><img src="/gaiban/images/okIcon.png" style="vertical-align:middle;" /> 验证成功</span></div>';
		if(arr[1].indexOf("实名认证") !== -1){
			htmlStr += '<img src="/images2/adv/sendSmsExp.gif" width="140" height="275" style="position:absolute;top:50px;right:20px;" />';
		}
		$("#feeSmsList").show().html(htmlStr);
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	// 2013-11-15 add by zhouqing -- begin
	else if(msg.indexOf('202') !== -1){
		return;
	}
	// -- end

	else {
		tip = '系统异常'
		sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
		return ;
	}
	getSmsBtn.hide();
	sendSmsTip.attr('innerHTML',tip);
	mobcheckcode.focus();

	countdowntime = time;
	intervalid = setInterval("count()",1000);
	$("#mobileHolder").addClass("hide");
	$("#mobcheckcode").focus();
}

// 2013-11-13 add by zhouqing -- begin
$("#hasSendBtn").live("click", function(){

	var $isChecking = $("#isChecking"),
	$hasSendBtn = $(this),
	$isCheckedErr = $("#isCheckedErr"),
	$isCheckedOk = $("#isCheckedOk");

	var lazyArr = [1000, 2000, 3000],
	lazyIdx = 0;

	var href = window.location.href,
	protocol = "http";
	if(href.indexOf("https") == 0){protocol = "https";}

	(function doCheck(){

		$hasSendBtn.hide();
		$isCheckedErr.hide();
		$isChecking.show();

		$.getJSON(
			protocol+"://reg.163.com/interfaces/urs/verifyUpSms.do?type=mibao2_replacemobile",
			//"/ftl/testData2/reg/hasSendSms.txt",
			function(data){
				$isChecking.hide();

				if(data.retCode-0 === 200){
					if(data.verifyStatus-0 === 1){
						$isCheckedOk.show();
						$("#mobcheckcode").val("000000");
						$("#upsms").removeAttr("disabled");
						$("input[type='submit']").trigger("click");
					}else{
						if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
							if(data.verifyStatus-0 === -1){
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。短信错误，请确认已经正确编辑短信内容。");
							}else{
								$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。系统未收到短信，请确认已经正确发送。");
							}
							$hasSendBtn.show();
							lazyIdx = 0;
						}else{
							$isChecking.show();
							setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
						}
					}
				}else{
					if(lazyIdx >= lazyArr.length){
						if(data.retCode-0 === 453){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("用户未绑定手机");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 412){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("验证失败。您今天尝试验证的次数过多，请改天再试。");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 500){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("系统异常");
						}else if(data.retCode-0 === 401){
							$isCheckedErr.show().text("传递的手机号错误");
						}
						$hasSendBtn.show();
						lazyIdx = 0;
					}else{
						$isChecking.show();
						setTimeout(doCheck, lazyArr[lazyIdx++]);
					}
				}
			}
		);
	})();
});
// -- end


</script>
